links() {\n return [\n {\n rel: \"canonical\",\n href: `https://example.com/produit/${params.id}/${params.slug}`\n }\n ];\n}\n\nexport default function ProductPage() {\n const { product } = useLoaderData();\n \n return (\n <>\n {/* Contenu de la page */}\n \n {/* JSON-LD pour les donnÃ©es structurÃ©es */}\n \n \n );\n}\n```\n\n## ğŸ§ª 4. Test et validation de la stratÃ©gie SEO\n\nPour garantir la prÃ©servation du rÃ©fÃ©rencement, un processus de test rigoureux est nÃ©cessaire:\n\n### Tests automatisÃ©s des URLs\n\n```typescript\n// gÃ©rÃ©es\nfor (const entry of urlMap) {\n test(`URL legacy: ${entry.legacy} â†’ nouvelle: ${entry.new}`, async ({ page }) => {\n // Tester la redirection\n await page.goto(entry.legacy);\n \n // Automatisation des tests\n\n### Configuration CI/CD\n\n```yaml\n# /.github/workflows/test.yml\n\nname: Test Suite\n\non:\n push:\n branches: [main, develop]\n pull_request:\n branches: [main, develop]\n\njobs:\n test:\n runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n\n services:\n postgres:\n image: postgres:14\n env:\n POSTGRES_USER: postgres\n POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres\n POSTGRES_DB: test_db\n ports:\n - 5432:5432\n options: >-\n --health-cmd pg_isready\n --health-interval 10s\n --health-timeout 5s\n --health-retries 5\n\n steps:\n - uses: actions/checkout@v3\n \n - name: Setup Node.js\n uses: actions/setup-node@v3\n with:\n node-version: '18'\n cache: 'npm'\n \n - name: Install dependencies\n run: npm ci\n \n - name: Generate Prisma client\n run: npx prisma generate\n \n - name: Setup test database\n run: npx prisma migrate deploy\n env:\n DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/test_db\n \n - name: Lint\n run: npm run lint\n \n - name: Unit Tests\n run: npm run test\n \n - name: Integration Tests\n run: npm run test:e2e\n env:\n DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/test_db\n \n - DÃ©ploiement progressif\n\n- Objectif : limiter les risques lors du passage en production\n- StratÃ©gies recommandÃ©es :\n - **Preview automatique** sur PR (Coolify, Vercel, Netlify, Renderâ€¦)\n - **Canary release** : 10% du trafic en premier, montÃ©e progressive\n - IntÃ©gration dans `ci-migration.yml`\n\n### StratÃ©gie de dÃ©ploiement progressif\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n A[Migration complÃ¨te] --> B[Environnement PR Preview]\n B --> C{Tests rÃ©ussis?}\n C -->|Non| D[Corrections]\n D --> B\n C -->|Oui| E[Staging]\n E --> F{Validation Staging?}\n F -->|Non| D\n F -->|Oui| G[Canary Release 10%]\n G --> H{MÃ©triques OK?}\n H -->|Non| I[Rollback]\n I --> D\n H -->|Oui| J[Canary 50%]\n J --> K{MÃ©triques OK?}\n K -->|Non| I\n K -->|Oui| L[DÃ©ploiement complet]\n L --> M[Surveillance continue]\n```\n\n### Configuration de preview automatique (Coolify)\n\n```yaml\n# /workspaces/cahier-des-charge/coolify.yml\nversion: \"3.7\"\nservices:\n api:\n build:\n context: .\n dockerfile: apps/api/Dockerfile\n environment:\n - NODE_ENV=preview\n - DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL}\n ports:\n - \"3000:3000\"\n healthcheck:\n test: [\"CMD\", \"curl\", \"-f\", \"http://localhost:3000/api/health\"]\n interval: 10s\n timeout: 5s\n retries: 3\n\n frontend:\n build:\n context: .\n dockerfile: apps/web/Dockerfile\n environment:\n - NODE_ENV=preview\n - API_URL=http://api:3000/api\n ports:\n - \"4000:4000\"\n depends_on:\n - api\n```\n\n### Mise en place de Canary Release\n\n```typescript\n// /workspaces/cahier-des-charge/scripts/deployment/canary-deploy.ts\nimport { DeploymentService } from './services/deployment';\nimport { MonitoringService } from './services/monitoring';\n\nasync function deployCanary(percentage: number) {\n console.log(`Starting canary deployment at ${percentage}% traffic...`);\n \n try {\n // 1. DÃ©ployer la nouvelle version en canary\n const deployment = await DeploymentService.deployCanary({\n version: process.env.VERSION || 'latest',\n trafficPercentage: percentage,\n environment: 'production',\n serviceName: 'api'\n });\n \n console.log(`Canary deployment ${deployment.id} initiated`);\n \n // 2. Surveiller les mÃ©triques pendant 15 minutes\n const monitoringDuration = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 minutes\n const monitoringInterval = 30 * 1000; // 30 secondes\n const startTime = Date.now();\n \n let stable = true;\n \n while (Date.now() - startTime < monitoringDuration) {\n console.log(`Monitoring canary deployment... (${Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 60000)}/${monitoringDuration/60000} minutes)`);\n \n // VÃ©rifier les mÃ©triques critiques\n const metrics = await MonitoringService.getCanaryMetrics(deployment.id);\n \n // CritÃ¨res d'Ã©chec\n if (\n metrics.errorRate > 1.0 || // Plus de 1% d'erreurs\n metrics.latencyP95 > 500 || // Latence P95 > 500ms\n metrics.cpu > 80 // Utilisation CPU > 80%\n ) {\n stable = false;\n console.error('Canary deployment unstable! Metrics:', metrics);\n break;\n }\n \n // Attendre avant la prochaine vÃ©rification\n await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, monitoringInterval));\n }\n \n if (stable) {\n console.log('Canary deployment successful!');\n \n if (percentage < 100) {\n console.log('Next step: increase traffic percentage or complete deployment');\n } else {\n console.log('Deployment complete!');\n \n // Nettoyage des anciennes versions\n await DeploymentService.cleanupOldVersions({\n keepCount: 2,\n environment: 'production',\n serviceName: 'api'\n });\n }\n \n return true;\n } else {\n console.error('Canary deployment failed! Rolling back...');\n \n // Rollback automatique\n await DeploymentService.rollback({\n deploymentId: deployment.id,\n environment: 'production',\n serviceName: 'api'\n });\n \n return false;\n }\n } catch (error) {\n console.error('Error during canary deployment:', error);\n return false;\n }\n}\n\n// ExÃ©cution avec le pourcentage spÃ©cifiÃ©\nconst targetPercentage = parseInt(process.argv[2], 10) || 10;\ndeployCanary(targetPercentage);\n```\n\n### IntÃ©gration dans le workflow CI/CD\n\n```yaml\n# /.github/workflows/ci-migration.yml\nname: CI/CD Migration\n\non:\n push:\n branches: [main]\n pull_request:\n branches: [main]\n\njobs:\n # Jobs de test et build omis pour concision\n \n preview:\n if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'\n needs: [test, build]\n runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n steps:\n - Surveillance continue\n\nLa surveillance post-dÃ©ploiement est cruciale pour dÃ©tecter rapidement les problÃ¨mes et maintenir la qualitÃ© de service.\n\n### MÃ©triques Ã  surveiller\n\n| CatÃ©gorie |
